\item 
Callable\mbox{[}\mbox{[}Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]}, Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]} \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1_a_p_i_router_a77e1de72bb9ddde47f413dbe72de8bf2}{get}} (self, Annotated\mbox{[}str, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The URL path to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}.                For example, in \`{}http\+://example.\+com/items\`{}, the path is \`{}/items\`{}.                "{}"{}"{}),\mbox{]} path, \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}, Annotated\mbox{[}Any, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for\+:                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation\+: the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization\+: you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering\+: the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation\+: whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Model\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/model/).                "{}"{}"{}),\mbox{]} response\+\_\+model=Default(None), Annotated\mbox{[}Optional\mbox{[}int\mbox{]}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1routing_1_1_router_aa6aaca9e4c478967705f74159bfcab2f}{default}} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code to be used for the response.                You could override the \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code by returning a response directly.                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Status Code\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}}-\/code/).                "{}"{}"{}),\mbox{]} status\+\_\+code=None, Annotated\mbox{[}Optional\mbox{[}List\mbox{[}Union\mbox{[}str, Enum\mbox{]}\mbox{]}\mbox{]}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                A list of \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1_a_p_i_router_acc5a0e0da5075b6576cc7e7000aa9a86}{tags}} to be applied to the \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}. \item 
Callable\mbox{[}\mbox{[}Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]}, Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]} \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1_a_p_i_router_adfb7e6a311d1f1f20b69b1606d9b6f0c}{put}} (self, Annotated\mbox{[}str, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The URL path to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}. "{}"{}"{}),\mbox{]} path, \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}, Annotated\mbox{[}Any, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for\+:                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation\+: the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization\+: you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering\+: the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation\+: whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Model\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/model/). \item 
Callable\mbox{[}\mbox{[}Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]}, Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]} \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1_a_p_i_router_ae7995c5d96aa805de2364c26d5fbe334}{post}} (self, Annotated\mbox{[}str, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The URL path to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}. "{}"{}"{}),\mbox{]} path, \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}, Annotated\mbox{[}Any, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for\+:                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation\+: the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization\+: you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering\+: the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation\+: whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Model\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/model/). \item 
Callable\mbox{[}\mbox{[}Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]}, Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]} \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1_a_p_i_router_a2740a7c5417d689ac9388030ee29b687}{delete}} (self, Annotated\mbox{[}str, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The URL path to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}. "{}"{}"{}),\mbox{]} path, \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}, Annotated\mbox{[}Any, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for\+:                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation\+: the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization\+: you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering\+: the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation\+: whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Model\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/model/). \item 
Callable\mbox{[}\mbox{[}Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]}, Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]} \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1_a_p_i_router_a478af6764f05157712a6effc1e77cc17}{patch}} (self, Annotated\mbox{[}str, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The URL path to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}. "{}"{}"{}),\mbox{]} path, \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}, Annotated\mbox{[}Any, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for\+:                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation\+: the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization\+: you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering\+: the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation\+: whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Model\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/model/). \item 
Callable\mbox{[}\mbox{[}Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]}, Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]} \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1_a_p_i_router_a66bbae042333b48f1488b8c5130e0ac5}{trace}} (self, Annotated\mbox{[}str, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The URL path to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}. "{}"{}"{}),\mbox{]} path, \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}, Annotated\mbox{[}Any, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for\+:                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation\+: the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization\+: you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering\+: the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation\+: whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Model\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/model/). When \`{}True\`{}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1routing_1_1_router_aa6aaca9e4c478967705f74159bfcab2f}{default}} values are omitted from the response.                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Model -\/ Return Type\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/model/\#use-\/the-\/response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+unset-\/parameter). This is much simpler (less smart) than \`{}response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+unset\`{}                and \`{}response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+defaults\`{}. \doxysubsection{Descripción detallada}
\begin{DoxyVerb}`APIRouter` class, used to group *path operations*, for example to structure
an app in multiple files. It would then be included in the `FastAPI` app, or
in another `APIRouter` (ultimately included in the app).

Read more about it in the
[FastAPI docs for Bigger Applications - Multiple Files](https://fastapi.tiangolo.com/tutorial/bigger-applications/).

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()


@router.get("/users/", tags=["users"])
async def read_users():
    return [{"username": "Rick"}, {"username": "Morty"}]


app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

"{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]}}]{path}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             Any,             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for\+:                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation\+: the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization\+: you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering\+: the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation\+: whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error). This is different from \`{}response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+unset\`{}                in that if the fields are set but contain the same \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1routing_1_1_router_aa6aaca9e4c478967705f74159bfcab2f}{default}} values,                they will be excluded from the response.                When \`{}True\`{}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1routing_1_1_router_aa6aaca9e4c478967705f74159bfcab2f}{default}} values are omitted from the response. "{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]} }]{response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+defaults}{ = {\ttfamily False}, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             bool,             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Configuration passed to Pydantic to define if the response data should                exclude fields set to \`{}None\`{}.                This is much simpler (less smart) than \`{}response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+unset\`{}                and \`{}response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+defaults\`{}. \begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP DELETE operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.delete("/items/{item_id}")
def delete_item(item_id: str):
    return {"message": "Item deleted"}

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

Hace referencia a \mbox{\hyperlink{fastapi_2routing_8py_source_l01070}{api\+\_\+route()}}.

It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for\+:                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation\+: the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization\+: you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering\+: the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation\+: whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error). \begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP GET operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.get("/items/")
def read_items():
    return [{"name": "Empanada"}, {"name": "Arepa"}]

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

"{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]}}]{path}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             Any,             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for\+:                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation\+: the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization\+: you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering\+: the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation\+: whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Model\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/model/). "{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]} }]{generate\+\_\+unique\+\_\+id\+\_\+function}{ = {\ttfamily Default(generate\+\_\+unique\+\_\+id)}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP HEAD operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI
from pydantic import BaseModel

class Item(BaseModel):
    name: str
    description: str | None = None

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.head("/items/", status_code=204)
def get_items_headers(response: Response):
    response.headers["X-Cat-Dog"] = "Alone in the world"

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Include another `APIRouter` in the same current `APIRouter`.

Read more about it in the
[FastAPI docs for Bigger Applications](https://fastapi.tiangolo.com/tutorial/bigger-applications/).

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI

app = FastAPI()
internal_router = APIRouter()
users_router = APIRouter()

@users_router.get("/users/")
def read_users():
    return [{"name": "Rick"}, {"name": "Morty"}]

internal_router.include_router(users_router)
app.include_router(internal_router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

\Hypertarget{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1_a_p_i_router_a5526a3962246dbc124d98956ea0d5f7a}\index{fastapi.routing.APIRouter@{fastapi.routing.APIRouter}!options@{options}}
\index{options@{options}!fastapi.routing.APIRouter@{fastapi.routing.APIRouter}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{options()}{options()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1_a_p_i_router_a5526a3962246dbc124d98956ea0d5f7a} 
 Callable\mbox{[}\mbox{[}Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]}, Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]} fastapi.\+routing.\+APIRouter.\+options (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             str,             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The URL path to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}.                For example, in \`{}http\+://example.\+com/items\`{}, the path is \`{}/items\`{}.                "{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]}}]{path}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             Any,             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for\+:                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation\+: the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization\+: you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering\+: the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation\+: whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Model\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/model/). \begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP OPTIONS operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.options("/items/")
def get_item_options():
    return {"additions": ["Aji", "Guacamole"]}

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

Hace referencia a \mbox{\hyperlink{fastapi_2routing_8py_source_l01070}{api\+\_\+route()}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{patch()}{patch()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1_a_p_i_router_a478af6764f05157712a6effc1e77cc17} 
 Callable\mbox{[}\mbox{[}Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]}, Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]} fastapi.\+routing.\+APIRouter.\+patch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             str,             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The URL path to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}.                For example, in \`{}http\+://example.\+com/items\`{}, the path is \`{}/items\`{}.                "{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]}}]{path}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             Any,             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for\+:                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation\+: the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization\+: you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering\+: the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation\+: whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Model\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/model/).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]} }]{response\+\_\+model}{ = {\ttfamily Default(None)}, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             Optional\mbox{[}int\mbox{]},             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1routing_1_1_router_aa6aaca9e4c478967705f74159bfcab2f}{default}} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code to be used for the response.                You could override the \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code by returning a response directly.                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Status Code\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}}-\/code/). \begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP PATCH operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI
from pydantic import BaseModel

class Item(BaseModel):
    name: str
    description: str | None = None

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.patch("/items/")
def update_item(item: Item):
    return {"message": "Item updated in place"}

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definición en la línea \mbox{\hyperlink{fastapi_2routing_8py_source_l03721}{3721}} del archivo \mbox{\hyperlink{fastapi_2routing_8py_source}{routing.\+py}}.



Hace referencia a \mbox{\hyperlink{fastapi_2routing_8py_source_l01070}{api\+\_\+route()}}.

 Callable\mbox{[}\mbox{[}Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]}, Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]} fastapi.\+routing.\+APIRouter.\+post (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             str,             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The URL path to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}.                For example, in \`{}http\+://example.\+com/items\`{}, the path is \`{}/items\`{}.                "{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]}}]{path}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             Any,             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for\+:                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation\+: the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization\+: you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering\+: the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation\+: whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Model\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/model/).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]} }]{response\+\_\+model}{ = {\ttfamily Default(None)}, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             Optional\mbox{[}int\mbox{]},             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1routing_1_1_router_aa6aaca9e4c478967705f74159bfcab2f}{default}} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code to be used for the response.                You could override the \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code by returning a response directly.                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Status Code\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}}-\/code/).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]} }]{status\+\_\+code}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             Optional\mbox{[}List\mbox{[}Union\mbox{[}str, Enum\mbox{]}\mbox{]}\mbox{]},             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                A list of \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1_a_p_i_router_acc5a0e0da5075b6576cc7e7000aa9a86}{tags}} to be applied to the \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}. \begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP POST operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI
from pydantic import BaseModel

class Item(BaseModel):
    name: str
    description: str | None = None

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.post("/items/")
def create_item(item: Item):
    return {"message": "Item created"}

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

Hace referencia a \mbox{\hyperlink{fastapi_2routing_8py_source_l01070}{api\+\_\+route()}}.

 Callable\mbox{[}\mbox{[}Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]}, Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]} fastapi.\+routing.\+APIRouter.\+put (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             str,             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The URL path to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}.                For example, in \`{}http\+://example.\+com/items\`{}, the path is \`{}/items\`{}.                "{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]}}]{path}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             Any,             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for\+:                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation\+: the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization\+: you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering\+: the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation\+: whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Model\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/model/).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]} }]{response\+\_\+model}{ = {\ttfamily Default(None)}, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             Optional\mbox{[}int\mbox{]},             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1routing_1_1_router_aa6aaca9e4c478967705f74159bfcab2f}{default}} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code to be used for the response.                You could override the \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code by returning a response directly. \begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP PUT operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI
from pydantic import BaseModel

class Item(BaseModel):
    name: str
    description: str | None = None

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.put("/items/{item_id}")
def replace_item(item_id: str, item: Item):
    return {"message": "Item replaced", "id": item_id}

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definición en la línea \mbox{\hyperlink{fastapi_2routing_8py_source_l01821}{1821}} del archivo \mbox{\hyperlink{fastapi_2routing_8py_source}{routing.\+py}}.



Hace referencia a \mbox{\hyperlink{fastapi_2routing_8py_source_l01070}{api\+\_\+route()}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1_a_p_i_router_a67b4cca1a170df82d069cc13570869eb} 
 Callable\mbox{[}\mbox{[}Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]}, Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]} fastapi.\+routing.\+APIRouter.\+route (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{str}]{path}{, }\item[{Optional\mbox{[}Collection\mbox{[}str\mbox{]}\mbox{]} }]{methods}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{Optional\mbox{[}str\mbox{]} }]{name}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{bool }]{include\+\_\+in\+\_\+schema}{ = {\ttfamily True}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}We no longer document this decorator style API, and its usage is discouraged.
Instead you should use the following approach:

>>> routes = [Route(path, endpoint=...), ...]
>>> app = Starlette(routes=routes)
\end{DoxyVerb}

 Callable\mbox{[}\mbox{[}Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]}, Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]} fastapi.\+routing.\+APIRouter.\+trace (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             str,             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The URL path to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}.                For example, in \`{}http\+://example.\+com/items\`{}, the path is \`{}/items\`{}.                "{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]}}]{path}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             Any,             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for\+:                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation\+: the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization\+: you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering\+: the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation\+: whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1_fast_a_p_i}{Fast\+API}} docs for \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1_response}{Response}} Model\mbox{]}(https\+://fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/tutorial/response-\/model/).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]} }]{response\+\_\+model}{ = {\ttfamily Default(None)}, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             Optional\mbox{[}int\mbox{]},             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The \mbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1routing_1_1_router_aa6aaca9e4c478967705f74159bfcab2f}{default}} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code to be used for the response.                You could override the \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code by returning a response directly. \begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP TRACE operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI
from pydantic import BaseModel

class Item(BaseModel):
    name: str
    description: str | None = None

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.trace("/items/{item_id}")
def trace_item(item_id: str):
    return None

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

"{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]}}]{path}{, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             Optional\mbox{[}str\mbox{]},             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                A name for the Web\+Socket. Only used internally.                "{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]} }]{name}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{Annotated\mbox{[}             Optional\mbox{[}Sequence\mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1params_1_1_depends}{params.\+Depends}}\mbox{]}\mbox{]},             \mbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1_doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                A list of \mbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1_a_p_i_router_a5b7a63684e1d513122740ca8ec0bc5a9}{dependencies}} (using \`{}Depends()\`{}) to be used for this                Web\+Socket. "{}"{}"{}             ),         \mbox{]} }]{dependencies}{ = {\ttfamily None}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Decorate a WebSocket function.

Read more about it in the
[FastAPI docs for WebSockets](https://fastapi.tiangolo.com/advanced/websockets/).

**Example**

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI, WebSocket

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.websocket("/ws")
async def websocket_endpoint(websocket: WebSocket):
    await websocket.accept()
    while True:
        data = await websocket.receive_text()
        await websocket.send_text(f"Message text was: {data}")

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1_a_p_i_router_a5f9330167494937a2e1196b21576a303} 
 Callable\mbox{[}\mbox{[}Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]}, Decorated\+Callable\mbox{]} fastapi.\+routing.\+APIRouter.\+websocket\+\_\+route (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{str}]{path}{, }\item[{Union\mbox{[}str, None\mbox{]} }]{name}{ = {\ttfamily None}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}We no longer document this decorator style API, and its usage is discouraged.
Instead you should use the following approach:

>>> routes = [WebSocketRoute(path, endpoint=...), ...]
>>> app = Starlette(routes=routes)
\end{DoxyVerb}
